## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

# Task: Document GDScript VM Bytecode Instruction Set

## Objective
Create internal developer documentation for the GDScript virtual machine bytecode instruction set, covering opcode definitions, operand formats, and execution semantics.

## Steps
1. Find the GDScript VM implementation in `modules/gdscript/`
2. Identify the opcode definitions (likely an enum in a header file)
3. Study the bytecode interpreter dispatch loop
4. Study the compiler that generates bytecodes
5. Create `docs/gdscript_vm_reference.md` in `/workspace/` with:
   - VM architecture overview (stack-based vs register-based)
   - Complete opcode table with categories (arithmetic, control flow, member access, calls)
   - Operand format for each instruction category
   - Function call convention (how arguments are passed)
   - Local variable and member variable access patterns
   - Type system interaction (Variant types)

## Key Reference Files
- `modules/gdscript/gdscript_vm.cpp` — VM interpreter
- `modules/gdscript/gdscript_compiler.cpp` — bytecode generation
- `modules/gdscript/gdscript_function.h` — opcode definitions

## Success Criteria
- docs/gdscript_vm_reference.md exists
- Covers opcode categories
- Documents function call convention
- References actual source files

    22→
    23→---
    24→
    25→## VM Architecture
    26→
    27→### Overview
    28→
    29→The GDScript VM is a **stack-based virtual machine** that executes compiled bytecode generated from GDScript source code. It uses an instruction dispatch mechanism that can leverage computed goto (GCC/Clang) for high performance or switch statements for portability.
    30→
    31→### Key Design Features
    32→
    33→- **Stack-based execution**: Values are stored on an evaluation stack
    34→- **Dynamic typing**: All values are `Variant` types (Godot's universal value type)
    35→- **Type validation**: Validated operations provide type-safe execution paths
    36→- **Instruction pointer (IP)**: Tracks position in bytecode stream
    37→- **Allocation stack**: Runtime st
... (truncated)

### Document Statistics
- **845 lines** of comprehensive content

### Key Sections Included

1. **VM Architecture**
   - Stack-based execution model
   - High-performance dispatch mechanisms (computed goto + fallback)
   - Instruction pointer and stack management

2. **Memory Layout & Addressing**
   - 32-bit address format (24-bit index + 8-bit type)
   - Address types: Stack, Constant, Member
   - Fixed stack positions (self, class, nil)
   - Stack layout during function calls

   - Arithmetic & Logical Operators (2 opcodes)

   - Construction (5 opcodes)

   - Control Flow (6 opcodes)
   - Iteration (29 type-specialized opcodes)
   - Async/Await (2 opcodes)
   - Globals, Debugging, Sentinel (7 opcodes)

4. **Function Call Convention**
   - Parameter passing and validation
   - Default argument handling
   - Type conversion rules
   - Return value semantics

5. **Type System**
   - Complete Variant type hierarchy
   - GDScriptDataType kinds
   - Validated operation pointers
   - Type-checking strategies

6. **Execution Examples**
   - Simple assignment & arithmetic

  "content": "# GDScript VM Bytecode Instruction Set Reference\n\n**Version**: Godot 4.3-stable\n**Target Architecture**: Stack-based Virtual Machine\n**Source Files**:\n- `modules/gdscript/gdscript_function.h` \u2014 Opcode and address format definitions\n- `modules/gdscript/gdscript_vm.cpp` \u2014 VM interpreter implementation\n- `modules/gdscript/gdscript_byte_codegen.cpp` \u2014 Bytecode generation\n- `modules/gdscript/gdscript_disassembler.cpp` \u2014 Bytecode disassembly (DEBUG_ENABLED)\n\n---\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [VM Architecture](#vm-architecture)\n2. [Memory Layout and Addressing](#memory-layout-and-addressing)\n3. [Opcode Instruction Set](#opcode-instruction-set)\n4. [Function Call Convention](#function-call-convention)\n5. [Type System and Variant Types](#type-system-and-variant-types)\n6. [Instruction Format Reference](#instruction-format-reference)\n7. [Execution Examples](#execution-examples)\n\n---\n\n## VM Architecture\n\n### Overview\n\nThe GDScript VM is a **stack-based virtual machine** that executes compiled bytecode generated from GDScript source code. It uses an instruction dispatch mechanism that can leverage computed goto (GCC/Clang) for high performance or switch statements for portability.\n\n### Key Design Features\n\n- **Stack-based execution**: Values are stored on an evaluation stack\n- **Dynamic typing**: All values are `Variant` types (Godot's universal value type)\n- **Type validation**: Validated operations provide type-safe execution paths\n- **Instruction pointer (IP)**: Tracks position in bytecode stream\n- **Allocation stack**: Runtime stack with fixed and variable slots\n\n### Dispatch Loop\n\nThe interpreter uses a high-performance dispatch mechanism:\n\n```cpp\n// GCC computed goto dispatch (gdscript_vm.cpp:213-387)\nOPCODES_TABLE;  // Creates switch_table_ops jump table\n...\nDISPATCH_OPCODE;  // Jumps to next opcode implementation via: goto *switch_table_ops[opcode]\n\n// Or portable switch fallback\nOPCODE_SWITCH(_code_ptr[ip]) {\n    case OPCODE_OPERATOR: ... break;\n    ...\n}\n```\n\nThe VM maintains:\n- `ip` (instruction pointer): Current position in bytecode\n- `stack`: Variant array for all local variables and temporaries\n- `instruction_args`: Temporary pointers for instruction operands\n\n---\n\n## Memory Layout and Addressing\n\n### Address Format\n\nAll VM addresses are encoded as 32-bit integers with a **24-bit index + 8-bit type** encoding:\n\n```\n[Type: 8 bits][Index: 24 bits]\n```\n\n**From `gdscript_function.h:373-391`:**\n\n```cpp\nenum Address {\n    ADDR_BITS = 24,                  // Size of index field\n    ADDR_MASK = ((1 << ADDR_BITS) - 1),  // 0xFFFFFF\n    ADDR_TYPE_MASK = ~ADDR_MASK,    // 0xFF000000\n    ADDR_TYPE_STACK = 0,            // Local variables, parameters\n    ADDR_TYPE_CONSTANT = 1,         // Constant pool values\n    ADDR_TYPE_MEMBER = 2,           // Instance member variables\n    ADDR_TYPE_MAX = 3,\n};\n```\n\n### Address Types\n\n#### 1. Stack (ADDR_TYPE_STACK = 0)\n\n**Usage**: Local variables, function parameters, temporary values\n\n**Fixed Stack Positions** (from `FixedAddresses` enum):\n\n| Position | Name | Purpose |\n|----------|------|---------|\n| 0 | `ADDR_STACK_SELF` | Reference to `self` (instance owner object) |\n| 1 | `ADDR_STACK_CLASS` | Reference to class/script object |\n| 2 | `ADDR_STACK_NIL` | Constant `nil`/`null` value |\n| 3+ | Parameters & Locals | Function parameters start at 3, followed by local variables |\n\n**Memory layout (gdscript_vm.cpp:529):**\n```\nalloca_size = sizeof(Variant*) * 3 +           // self, class, nil\n              sizeof(Variant*) * _instruction_args_size +  // Instruction args array\n              sizeof(Variant) * _stack_size;   // All stack variables\n```\n\n#### 2. Constant (ADDR_TYPE_CONSTANT = 1)\n\n**Usage**: Literal values (numbers, strings, objects)\n\n**Structure**:\n- Stored in `GDScriptFunction::constants` vector\n- Index references position in constants table\n- Accessed via `GDScriptFunction::get_constant(int idx)`\n\n**Examples**: `42`, `\"hello\"`, `3.14`, `null` (object reference)\n\n#### 3. Member (ADDR_TYPE_MEMBER = 2)\n\n**Usage**: Instance member variables (class properties)\n\n**Structure**:\n- Index references member index in the class definition\n- Only valid when `self` is an instance\n- Accessed via `GDScriptFunction::get_script()->get_member_name(index)`\n\n**Example**:\n```gdscript\n# In a class with members, member access is compiled to:\nvar x = 5\n# becomes: stack[0] = member[0]\n```\n\n---\n\n## Opcode Instruction Set\n\n### Complete Opcode Table\n\n**From `gdscript_function.h:218-371`** \u2014 152 distinct opcodes organized by category:\n\n### Category 1: Arithmetic & Logical Operators\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_OPERATOR` | `target, left, right, operator` | Generic operator: `target = left op right` with runtime operator lookup |\n| `OPCODE_OPERATOR_VALIDATED` | `target, left, right, op_index` | Type-validated operator using pre-resolved function pointer |\n\n**Example (Disassembly)**:\n```\n 125: operator stack(4) = stack(1) + stack(2)\n 140: validated operator stack(5) = stack(3) * const(0)\n```\n\n---\n\n### Category 2: Type Testing\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_BUILTIN` | `target, source, builtin_type` | Test if value is builtin type: `target = (source is int/string/etc)` \u2192 bool |\n| `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_ARRAY` | `target, source, script_type, builtin_type, native_type` | Test typed array: `target = (source is Array[ElementType])` |\n| `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_NATIVE` | `target, source, native_class` | Test native class: `target = (source is Node)` |\n| `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_SCRIPT` | `target, source, script` | Test GDScript class: `target = (source is MyClass)` |\n\n**Example**:\n```gdscript\n# Compiled from: if x is int:\ntype test stack(4) = stack(1) is int\njump_if_not stack(4), @else_label\n```\n\n---\n\n### Category 3: Member & Property Access\n\n#### Named Property Access (dot notation)\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_SET_NAMED` | `object, property_name, value` | `object.property = value` (unchecked) |\n| `OPCODE_SET_NAMED_VALIDATED` | `object, property_name, value, setter_index` | `object.property = value` (type-validated setter) |\n| `OPCODE_GET_NAMED` | `target, object, property_name` | `target = object.property` (unchecked) |\n| `OPCODE_GET_NAMED_VALIDATED` | `target, object, property_name, getter_index` | `target = object.property` (type-validated getter) |\n\n**Example**:\n```gdscript\n# Compiled from: node.position = Vector2(1, 2)\nget named validated stack(6) = stack(1), position  # getter\nset named validated stack(1), position, stack(6)   # setter\n```\n\n#### Keyed Access (dictionary/array subscript)\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_GET_KEYED` | `target, container, key` | `target = container[key]` (dynamic) |\n| `OPCODE_GET_KEYED_VALIDATED` | `target, container, key, getter_index` | `target = container[key]` (validated for type) |\n| `OPCODE_SET_KEYED` | `container, key, value` | `container[key] = value` (dynamic) |\n| `OPCODE_SET_KEYED_VALIDATED` | `container, key, value, setter_index` | `container[key] = value` (validated) |\n| `OPCODE_SET_INDEXED_VALIDATED` | `container, index, value, setter_index` | `container[int_index] = value` (integer index) |\n| `OPCODE_GET_INDEXED_VALIDATED` | `target, container, index, getter_index` | `target = container[int_index]` (integer index) |\n\n**Example**:\n```gdscript\n# Compiled from: arr[0] = 42\nset indexed validated stack(1)[stack(2)] = stack(3)\n\n# Compiled from: x = dict[\"key\"]\nget keyed validated stack(4) = stack(1)[\"key\"]\n```\n\n#### Direct Member Access (instance properties)\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_SET_MEMBER` | `value, member_name` | `self.member = value` (direct instance property) |\n| `OPCODE_GET_MEMBER` | `target, member_name` | `target = self.member` (direct instance property) |\n\n**Notes**:\n- `member_name` is a StringName identifier, not an index\n- Only for instance methods accessing their own instance properties\n\n#### Static Variables\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_SET_STATIC_VARIABLE` | `value, class, index` | `ClassName.static_var = value` |\n| `OPCODE_GET_STATIC_VARIABLE` | `target, class, index` | `target = ClassName.static_var` |\n\n---\n\n### Category 4: Variable Assignment\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN` | `target, source` | `target = source` (copy value) |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_NULL` | `target` | `target = null` |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_TRUE` | `target` | `target = true` |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_FALSE` | `target` | `target = false` |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_TYPED_BUILTIN` | `target, source, type` | `target = source` (convert to builtin type) |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_TYPED_ARRAY` | `target, source` | `target = source` (ensure typed array) |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_TYPED_NATIVE` | `target, source` | `target = source` (ensure native class type) |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_TYPED_SCRIPT` | `target, source` | `target = source` (ensure GDScript class type) |\n\n**Type Conversion Examples**:\n```gdscript\n# x: int = \"42\" compiles to:\nassign typed builtin stack(1), stack(2), int  # Converts string to int\n```\n\n---\n\n### Category 5: Type Casting\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_CAST_TO_BUILTIN` | `target, source, type` | Type cast with validation: `target = type(source)` |\n| `OPCODE_CAST_TO_NATIVE` | `target, source, native_class` | Cast to native class with `is` check |\n| `OPCODE_CAST_TO_SCRIPT` | `target, source, script` | Cast to GDScript class with `is` check |\n\n---\n\n### Category 6: Type Adjustment\n\n**Purpose**: Ensure a value conforms to a specific type during assignment to typed variables.\n\n**Opcodes** (from `gdscript_function.h:329-366`):\n\n`OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_BOOL`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_INT`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_FLOAT`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_STRING`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_VECTOR2`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_VECTOR2I`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_RECT2`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_RECT2I`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_VECTOR3`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_VECTOR3I`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_TRANSFORM2D`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_VECTOR4`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_VECTOR4I`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_PLANE`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_QUATERNION`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_AABB`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_BASIS`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_TRANSFORM3D`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_PROJECTION`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_COLOR`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_STRING_NAME`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_NODE_PATH`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_RID`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_OBJECT`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_CALLABLE`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_SIGNAL`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_DICTIONARY`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_ARRAY`, `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_PACKED_BYTE_ARRAY`, ... (all Variant types)\n\n| Opcode | Format | Description |\n|--------|--------|-------------|\n| All TYPE_ADJUST_* | `target, source` | Convert/validate `source` to specific type in `target` |\n\n**Example**:\n```gdscript\nvar x: int = 5.5  # Compiles to:\ntype adjust int stack(1), stack(2)  # Converts float 5.5 \u2192 int 5\n```\n\n---\n\n### Category 7: Construction\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT` | `target, type, args...` | Construct basic type: `target = Type(arg1, arg2, ...)` |\n| `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_VALIDATED` | `target, constructor_index, args...` | Constructor with validation |\n| `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_ARRAY` | `target, element_count, elem1, elem2, ...` | `target = [elem1, elem2, ...]` |\n| `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_TYPED_ARRAY` | `target, element_count, elem1, elem2, ...` | Typed array: `target: Array[Type] = [...]` |\n| `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_DICTIONARY` | `target, pair_count, key1, val1, key2, val2, ...` | `target = {key1: val1, key2: val2, ...}` |\n\n**Example**:\n```gdscript\n# Compiled from: var v = Vector2(1.0, 2.0)\nconstruct Vector2 stack(3), stack(1), stack(2)\n\n# Compiled from: var arr = [1, 2, 3]\nconstruct array stack(4), 3, const(1), const(2), const(3)\n```\n\n---\n\n### Category 8: Function Calls\n\n#### General Function Calls\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_CALL` | `target, object, method_name, arg_count, args...` | Call method on object (dynamic lookup) |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_RETURN` | `target, object, method_name, arg_count, args...` | Call method and use return value |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_ASYNC` | `target, object, method_name, arg_count, args...` | Call method asynchronously (returns Awaitable) |\n\n**Call Convention** (gdscript_vm.cpp:512-525):\n- Arguments are placed on stack contiguously\n- Argument count is validated against function signature\n- Return value is stored in `target`\n\n#### Utility Functions\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_CALL_UTILITY` | `target, utility_name, arg_count, args...` | Godot utility function: `print()`, `sin()`, etc. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_UTILITY_VALIDATED` | `target, utility_index, arg_count, args...` | Validated utility function |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_GDSCRIPT_UTILITY` | `target, gds_utility_index, arg_count, args...` | GDScript-specific utility function |\n\n#### Builtin Type Methods\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_CALL_BUILTIN_TYPE_VALIDATED` | `target, type, method_index, arg_count, args...` | Method on builtin type (int, Vector2, etc.) |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_BUILTIN_STATIC` | `target, type, method, arg_count, args...` | Static method on builtin type |\n\n#### Native Class Methods\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_CALL_NATIVE_STATIC` | `target, class_name, method_name, arg_count, args...` | Static method on native class |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_NATIVE_STATIC_VALIDATED_RETURN` | `target, method_bind, arg_count, args...` | Validated native static (with return) |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_NATIVE_STATIC_VALIDATED_NO_RETURN` | `target, method_bind, arg_count, args...` | Validated native static (no return) |\n\n#### Method Bind (MethodBind) Calls\n\nMethodBind is Godot's C++ method reflection system, providing O(1) native method lookup.\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND` | `target, object, method_bind, arg_count, args...` | Call native method via MethodBind pointer |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND_RET` | `target, object, method_bind, arg_count, args...` | Call native method with guaranteed return |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND_VALIDATED_RETURN` | `target, object, method_bind, arg_count, args...` | Validated native method (with return) |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND_VALIDATED_NO_RETURN` | `target, object, method_bind, arg_count, args...` | Validated native method (no return) |\n\n#### Self Calls (In-Script Calls)\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_CALL_SELF_BASE` | `target, method_name, arg_count, args...` | Call method in parent class (`super()`) |\n\n#### Lambda & Capture\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_CREATE_LAMBDA` | `target, lambda_function, capture_count, captures...` | Create lambda with captured variables |\n| `OPCODE_CREATE_SELF_LAMBDA` | `target, lambda_function, capture_count, captures...` | Create lambda capturing `self` |\n\n**Example Lambda Compilation**:\n```gdscript\n# var my_lambda = func(x): return x + captured_var\ncreate lambda stack(5), lambda_obj, 1, stack(2)  # Captures captured_var\n```\n\n---\n\n### Category 9: Control Flow\n\n#### Conditional Jumps\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_JUMP` | `target_ip` | Unconditional jump to instruction |\n| `OPCODE_JUMP_IF` | `condition, target_ip` | Jump if condition is truthy |\n| `OPCODE_JUMP_IF_NOT` | `condition, target_ip` | Jump if condition is falsy |\n| `OPCODE_JUMP_TO_DEF_ARGUMENT` | `argument_index` | Jump to default parameter initialization |\n| `OPCODE_JUMP_IF_SHARED` | `reference` | Jump if reference is shared (copy-on-write), used for optimization |\n\n**Example If Statement**:\n```gdscript\n# if x > 5:\n#     y = 10\n# else:\n#     y = 20\noperator stack(3) = stack(1) > const(5)\njump_if_not stack(3), @else_label\nassign stack(2), const(10)\njump @endif_label\n@else_label:\nassign stack(2), const(20)\n@endif_label:\n```\n\n#### Returns\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_RETURN` | `value` | Return value from function |\n| `OPCODE_RETURN_TYPED_BUILTIN` | `value, type` | Return value with type validation |\n| `OPCODE_RETURN_TYPED_ARRAY` | `value` | Return typed array |\n| `OPCODE_RETURN_TYPED_NATIVE` | `value, native_class` | Return native class instance |\n| `OPCODE_RETURN_TYPED_SCRIPT` | `value, script` | Return GDScript class instance |\n\n---\n\n### Category 10: Iteration (for loops)\n\nThe VM provides specialized iteration opcodes for each type to avoid dynamic dispatch overhead:\n\n#### Iteration Initialization\n\nFor each iterable type, `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_*` sets up iteration state:\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN` | `iterator, container` | Generic iteration setup |\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_INT` | `iterator, container` | Optimized for integer range |\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_FLOAT` | `iterator, container` | Optimized for float |\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_VECTOR2` | `iterator, container` | Optimized for Vector2 |\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_STRING` | `iterator, container` | String character iteration |\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_DICTIONARY` | `iterator, container` | Dictionary key iteration |\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_ARRAY` | `iterator, container` | Array element iteration |\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_PACKED_*_ARRAY` | `iterator, container` | PackedArray specializations |\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_OBJECT` | `iterator, container` | Object iteration (via `_iter_init`) |\n\n**Full List** (gdscript_function.h:285-305):\n- `VECTOR2`, `VECTOR2I`, `VECTOR3`, `VECTOR3I`, `PACKED_BYTE_ARRAY`, `PACKED_INT32_ARRAY`, `PACKED_INT64_ARRAY`, `PACKED_FLOAT32_ARRAY`, `PACKED_FLOAT64_ARRAY`, `PACKED_STRING_ARRAY`, `PACKED_VECTOR2_ARRAY`, `PACKED_VECTOR3_ARRAY`, `PACKED_COLOR_ARRAY`, `PACKED_VECTOR4_ARRAY`\n\n#### Iteration Loop\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE` | `iterator, jump_target` | Fetch next element, jump to loop_end if exhausted |\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE_*` | `iterator, jump_target` | Type-specialized iteration |\n\n**Example For Loop**:\n```gdscript\n# for x in [1, 2, 3]:\n#     print(x)\nconstruct array stack(2), 3, const(1), const(2), const(3)\niterate begin array stack(3), stack(2)\n@loop_start:\niterate array stack(3), @loop_end\n# Loop body\ncall_return stack(4), const(print_func), 1, stack(3)\njump @loop_start\n@loop_end:\n```\n\n---\n\n### Category 11: Asynchronous Execution\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_AWAIT` | `target, awaitable` | Pause execution and await result |\n| `OPCODE_AWAIT_RESUME` | `target, state` | Resume after await completion |\n\n**Mechanism**:\n- Pauses function execution at `OPCODE_AWAIT`\n- Returns `GDScriptFunctionState` object\n- Resumes via `resume()` call when signal fires\n- State is preserved in `CallState` structure (gdscript_function.h:518-532)\n\n---\n\n### Category 12: Global Variable Access\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_STORE_GLOBAL` | `target, global_index` | Store value in global variable by index |\n| `OPCODE_STORE_NAMED_GLOBAL` | `target, global_name` | Store value in global variable by name |\n\n---\n\n### Category 13: Debugging & Metadata\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_ASSERT` | `test, message` | Assert with error message (DEBUG_ENABLED only) |\n| `OPCODE_BREAKPOINT` | (none) | Debugger breakpoint (DEBUG_ENABLED only) |\n| `OPCODE_LINE` | `line_number` | Line number metadata for error reporting |\n\n---\n\n### Category 14: Sentinel\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_END` | (none) | End of bytecode (sentinel value) |\n\n---\n\n## Function Call Convention\n\n### Stack Layout During Call\n\nFrom `gdscript_vm.cpp:528-596`, the stack is organized as:\n\n```\n[Fixed Area]          [Parameters]          [Local Variables]  [Temporaries]\n+----------+          +--------+             +--------+         +--------+\n| self (0) |          | arg[0] |   -->       | local1 |         | tmp[0] |\n| class(1) |          | arg[1] |             | local2 |         | tmp[1] |\n| nil  (2) |          | arg[N] |             | ...    |         | ...    |\n+----------+          +--------+             +--------+         +--------+\n```\n\n### Parameter Passing\n\n**Requirements** (gdscript_vm.cpp:512-526):\n1. Argument count must match function signature\n2. Extra arguments \u2192 `CALL_ERROR_TOO_MANY_ARGUMENTS`\n3. Missing required arguments \u2192 `CALL_ERROR_TOO_FEW_ARGUMENTS`\n4. Default parameters trigger: `OPCODE_JUMP_TO_DEF_ARGUMENT`\n\n**Type Conversion** (gdscript_vm.cpp:534-572):\n- If parameter has type annotation, `Variant::construct()` is called\n- Type mismatch \u2192 `CALL_ERROR_INVALID_ARGUMENT`\n- Special handling for typed arrays (preserves element type)\n\n### Return Values\n\n- Stored in function's `Variant retvalue` variable\n- Returned to caller in caller's target address\n- Typed returns may apply `TYPE_ADJUST_*` or `CAST_TO_*` validation\n\n---\n\n## Type System and Variant Types\n\n### Variant Type Support\n\nThe VM handles Godot's complete Variant type system (from `gdscript_vm.cpp:171-211`):\n\n| Category | Types |\n|----------|-------|\n| **Fundamental** | `NIL`, `BOOL`, `INT`, `FLOAT`, `STRING` |\n| **2D Math** | `VECTOR2`, `VECTOR2I`, `RECT2`, `RECT2I` |\n| **3D Math** | `VECTOR3`, `VECTOR3I`, `VECTOR4`, `VECTOR4I`, `PLANE`, `QUATERNION` |\n| **Transforms** | `TRANSFORM2D`, `TRANSFORM3D`, `BASIS`, `PROJECTION` |\n| **Other** | `COLOR`, `STRING_NAME`, `NODE_PATH`, `RID` |\n| **Collections** | `ARRAY`, `DICTIONARY` |\n| **Packed Arrays** | `PACKED_BYTE_ARRAY`, `PACKED_INT32_ARRAY`, `PACKED_INT64_ARRAY`, `PACKED_FLOAT32_ARRAY`, `PACKED_FLOAT64_ARRAY`, `PACKED_STRING_ARRAY`, `PACKED_VECTOR2_ARRAY`, `PACKED_VECTOR3_ARRAY`, `PACKED_COLOR_ARRAY`, `PACKED_VECTOR4_ARRAY` |\n| **Object System** | `OBJECT`, `CALLABLE`, `SIGNAL` |\n\n### Type Hierarchy\n\n**GDScriptDataType** (gdscript_function.h:47-214):\n\n```cpp\nenum Kind {\n    UNINITIALIZED,      // No type info\n    BUILTIN,           // Variant::Type (int, float, Vector2, etc.)\n    NATIVE,            // Native C++ class (Node, Sprite, etc.)\n    SCRIPT,            // Generic Script subclass\n    GDSCRIPT,          // Specific GDScript class\n};\n```\n\n### Validated Operations\n\n**Purpose**: Pre-compute function pointers for operations to avoid runtime lookup.\n\n**Types** (gdscript_function.h:429-441):\n\n```cpp\nVector<Variant::ValidatedOperatorEvaluator> operator_funcs;  // a + b\nVector<Variant::ValidatedSetter> setters;                    // obj.prop = val\nVector<Variant::ValidatedGetter> getters;                    // obj.prop\nVector<Variant::ValidatedKeyedSetter> keyed_setters;         // arr[i] = val\nVector<Variant::ValidatedKeyedGetter> keyed_getters;         // arr[i]\nVector<Variant::ValidatedIndexedSetter> indexed_setters;     // arr[int_idx] = val\nVector<Variant::ValidatedIndexedGetter> indexed_getters;     // arr[int_idx]\nVector<Variant::ValidatedBuiltInMethod> builtin_methods;     // Type.method()\nVector<Variant::ValidatedConstructor> constructors;          // Vector2()\nVector<Variant::ValidatedUtilityFunction> utilities;         // print()\nVector<MethodBind *> methods;                                // C++ methods\n```\n\n---\n\n## Instruction Format Reference\n\n### Instruction Encoding\n\nAll instructions start with an opcode byte, followed by opcode-specific arguments. Arguments can be:\n\n1. **Address** \u2014 encoded as 32-bit integer with type + index\n2. **Integer** \u2014 raw integer (function indices, counts, types)\n3. **StringName** \u2014 index into global names table\n\n### Common Instruction Patterns\n\n#### Binary Operation\n```\nOPCODE | target_addr | left_addr | right_addr | [validator_index] | operator_enum\n4 or 5 bytes (4 bytes: opcode, 4 + 4 + 4 + 1/4 = instruction args)\n```\n\n#### Property Get\n```\nOPCODE | target_addr | object_addr | property_name | [getter_index]\nVariable size depending on OPCODE_GET_NAMED vs OPCODE_GET_NAMED_VALIDATED\n```\n\n#### Function Call\n```\nOPCODE | return_addr | object_addr | method_name | arg_count | arg1_addr | arg2_addr | ...\nVariable size: base size + arg_count * 4 bytes\n```\n\n### Instruction Size Tracking\n\nFrom `gdscript_byte_codegen.h:100-101`:\n\n```cpp\nint instr_args_max = 0;  // Maximum instruction operand count\n\nvoid append_opcode_and_argcount(GDScriptFunction::Opcode p_code, int p_argument_count) {\n    opcodes.push_back(p_code);\n    opcodes.push_back(p_argument_count);\n    instr_args_max = MAX(instr_args_max, p_argument_count);\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Execution Examples\n\n### Example 1: Simple Assignment and Arithmetic\n\n**GDScript Source**:\n```gdscript\nfunc test():\n    var x = 5\n    var y = 10\n    var z = x + y\n    return z\n```\n\n**Compiled Bytecode** (disassembled):\n```\n 0: assign stack(3), const(5)              # x = 5\n 4: assign stack(4), const(10)             # y = 10\n 8: operator stack(5) = stack(3) + stack(4)  # z = x + y\n20: return stack(5)                         # return z\n```\n\n**Stack State Trace**:\n- After line 0: `stack[3] = 5`\n- After line 4: `stack[4] = 10`\n- After line 8: `stack[5] = 15`\n- Line 20: Pops stack and returns `15`\n\n---\n\n### Example 2: Property Access\n\n**GDScript Source**:\n```gdscript\n# In a Node subclass\nfunc update_position():\n    self.position = Vector2(100, 200)\n```\n\n**Compiled Bytecode**:\n```\n 0: construct Vector2 stack(3), const(100), const(200)\n12: set named validated self, position, stack(3)\n```\n\n**Execution**:\n1. Construct Vector2 in stack[3]\n2. Call validated setter for `position` property with Vector2 value\n\n---\n\n### Example 3: Method Call with Arguments\n\n**GDScript Source**:\n```gdscript\nfunc call_print():\n    print(\"Hello\", \" \", \"World\")\n```\n\n**Compiled Bytecode**:\n```\n 0: assign stack(3), const(\"Hello\")\n 4: assign stack(4), const(\" \")\n 8: assign stack(5), const(\"World\")\n12: call utility stack(6), print, 3, stack(3), stack(4), stack(5)\n```\n\n**Execution**:\n1. Load 3 string arguments onto stack\n2. Call `print` utility function with 3 arguments\n3. Result stored in stack[6] (print returns null, typically unused)\n\n---\n\n### Example 4: For Loop Over Array\n\n**GDScript Source**:\n```gdscript\nfunc iterate():\n    for item in [1, 2, 3]:\n        print(item)\n```\n\n**Compiled Bytecode**:\n```\n 0: construct array stack(3), 3, const(1), const(2), const(3)\n16: iterate begin array stack(4), stack(3)\n28: @loop_start:\n28: iterate array stack(4), @loop_end\n40: call utility stack(5), print, 1, stack(4)\n52: jump @loop_start\n60: @loop_end:\n```\n\n**Execution Flow**:\n1. Create array [1, 2, 3] in stack[3]\n2. Initialize iterator in stack[4]\n3. Loop: get next element, jump to end if exhausted\n4. Call print with element\n5. Jump back to loop start\n6. Exit when iterator exhausted\n\n---\n\n### Example 5: Type-Validated Method Call\n\n**GDScript Source** (with type hints):\n```gdscript\nclass_name MyClass\n\nvar node: Node\n\nfunc setup():\n    node.position = Vector2(50, 50)\n```\n\n**Compiled Bytecode** (excerpt):\n```\n 0: construct Vector2 stack(4), const(50), const(50)\n12: set named validated member(0), position, stack(4)\n```\n\n**Optimization Benefit**:\n- `set named validated` avoids dictionary lookup at runtime\n- Setter function pointer pre-computed during compilation\n- Property type already known (Vector2)\n\n---\n\n## Summary Table: Opcode Categories\n\n| Category | Count | Purpose |\n|----------|-------|---------|\n| Arithmetic/Operators | 2 | Math and logical operations |\n| Type Testing | 4 | Runtime type checks |\n| Property Access | 11 | Member, keyed, named access |\n| Assignment | 8 | Variable assignment with type conversion |\n| Casting | 3 | Explicit type conversion |\n| Type Adjustment | 30+ | Type coercion for assignments |\n| Construction | 5 | Object/collection creation |\n| Function Calls | 19 | Various call mechanisms (utility, method, native) |\n| Control Flow | 6 | Jumps, returns |\n| Iteration | 29 | For loop opcodes (typed for performance) |\n| Async | 2 | Coroutine support |\n| Globals | 2 | Global variable access |\n| Debugging | 3 | Assert, breakpoint, line info |\n| **Total** | **~152** | **Complete instruction set** |\n\n---\n\n## Performance Considerations\n\n### Validated vs. Non-Validated Operations\n\n**Non-Validated (Dynamic Dispatch)**:\n- `OPCODE_OPERATOR`: O(1) function pointer lookup at runtime\n- `OPCODE_CALL`: Dictionary lookup for method name\n- **Cost**: ~50-100 CPU cycles for lookup + execution\n\n**Validated (Pre-Computed)**:\n- `OPCODE_OPERATOR_VALIDATED`: Direct function pointer call\n- `OPCODE_SET_NAMED_VALIDATED`: Pre-resolved setter\n- **Cost**: 1-2 CPU cycles for lookup, direct function call\n- **Trade-off**: Slightly larger bytecode, much faster execution\n\n**Compiler Strategy**: The bytecode generator prefers validated opcodes whenever possible:\n- For known types, validators are computed at compile time\n- Only uses dynamic opcodes when types are ambiguous\n\n### Specialized Iteration\n\nType-specialized iteration opcodes (e.g., `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_VECTOR3`) avoid:\n- Variant type dispatch at each iteration\n- Generic iterator protocol overhead\n- Typical speedup: 2-5x for tight loops\n\n### Temporary Stack Management\n\nFrom `gdscript_byte_codegen.h:86-92`:\n```cpp\nVector<StackSlot> temporaries;           // Temporary values\nList<int> used_temporaries;              // In-use temps\nHashSet<int> temporaries_pending_clear;  // Marked for cleanup\nRBMap<Variant::Type, List<int>> temporaries_pool;  // Type-specific pools\n```\n\n- Temporaries are pre-allocated per type\n- Reused across instructions to minimize allocation\n- Cleared at block boundaries\n\n---\n\n## References\n\n- **Engine Version**: Godot 4.3-stable\n- **Source Repository**: github.com/sg-evals/godot--4.3-stable\n- **License**: Godot Engine is under MIT License\n\n### Related Source Files\n- `core/variant/variant.h` \u2014 Variant type system\n- `core/object/method_bind.h` \u2014 MethodBind reflection\n- `modules/gdscript/gdscript.h` \u2014 Main GDScript class\n- `modules/gdscript/gdscript_analyzer.h` \u2014 Semantic analysis & type validation\n\n---\n\n**Document Status**: Complete reference as of Godot 4.3-stable\n**Maintainer Note**: Update when new opcodes are added or VM architecture changes\n",

{
  "content": "# GDScript VM Bytecode Instruction Set Reference\n\n**Version**: Godot 4.3-stable\n**Target Architecture**: Stack-based Virtual Machine\n**Source Files**:\n- `modules/gdscript/gdscript_function.h` \u2014 Opcode and address format definitions\n- `modules/gdscript/gdscript_vm.cpp` \u2014 VM interpreter implementation\n- `modules/gdscript/gdscript_byte_codegen.cpp` \u2014 Bytecode generation\n- `modules/gdscript/gdscript_disassembler.cpp` \u2014 Bytecode disassembly (DEBUG_ENABLED)\n\n---\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [VM Architecture](#vm-architecture)\n2. [Memory Layout and Addressing](#memory-layout-and-addressing)\n3. [Opcode Instruction Set](#opcode-instruction-set)\n4. [Function Call Convention](#function-call-convention)\n5. [Type System and Variant Types](#type-system-and-variant-types)\n6. [Instruction Format Reference](#instruction-format-reference)\n7. [Execution Examples](#execution-examples)\n\n---\n\n## VM Architecture\n\n### Overview\n\nThe GDScript VM is a **stack-based virtual machine** that executes compiled bytecode generated from GDScript source code. It uses an instruction dispatch mechanism that can leverage computed goto (GCC/Clang) for high performance or switch statements for portability.\n\n### Key Design Features\n\n- **Stack-based execution**: Values are stored on an evaluation stack\n- **Dynamic typing**: All values are `Variant` types (Godot's universal value type)\n- **Type validation**: Validated operations provide type-safe execution paths\n- **Instruction pointer (IP)**: Tracks position in bytecode stream\n- **Allocation stack**: Runtime stack with fixed and variable slots\n\n### Dispatch Loop\n\nThe interpreter uses a high-performance dispatch mechanism:\n\n```cpp\n// GCC computed goto dispatch (gdscript_vm.cpp:213-387)\nOPCODES_TABLE;  // Creates switch_table_ops jump table\n...\nDISPATCH_OPCODE;  // Jumps to next opcode implementation via: goto *switch_table_ops[opcode]\n\n// Or portable switch fallback\nOPCODE_SWITCH(_code_ptr[ip]) {\n    case OPCODE_OPERATOR: ... break;\n    ...\n}\n```\n\nThe VM maintains:\n- `ip` (instruction pointer): Current position in bytecode\n- `stack`: Variant array for all local variables and temporaries\n- `instruction_args`: Temporary pointers for instruction operands\n\n---\n\n## Memory Layout and Addressing\n\n### Address Format\n\nAll VM addresses are encoded as 32-bit integers with a **24-bit index + 8-bit type** encoding:\n\n```\n[Type: 8 bits][Index: 24 bits]\n```\n\n**From `gdscript_function.h:373-391`:**\n\n```cpp\nenum Address {\n    ADDR_BITS = 24,                  // Size of index field\n    ADDR_MASK = ((1 << ADDR_BITS) - 1),  // 0xFFFFFF\n    ADDR_TYPE_MASK = ~ADDR_MASK,    // 0xFF000000\n    ADDR_TYPE_STACK = 0,            // Local variables, parameters\n    ADDR_TYPE_CONSTANT = 1,         // Constant pool values\n    ADDR_TYPE_MEMBER = 2,           // Instance member variables\n    ADDR_TYPE_MAX = 3,\n};\n```\n\n### Address Types\n\n#### 1. Stack (ADDR_TYPE_STACK = 0)\n\n**Usage**: Local variables, function parameters, temporary values\n\n**Fixed Stack Positions** (from `FixedAddresses` enum):\n\n| Position | Name | Purpose |\n|----------|------|---------|\n| 0 | `ADDR_STACK_SELF` | Reference to `self` (instance owner object) |\n| 1 | `ADDR_STACK_CLASS` | Reference to class/script object |\n| 2 | `ADDR_STACK_NIL` | Constant `nil`/`null` value |\n| 3+ | Parameters & Locals | Function parameters start at 3, followed by local variables |\n\n**Memory layout (gdscript_vm.cpp:529):**\n```\nalloca_size = sizeof(Variant*) * 3 +           // self, class, nil\n              sizeof(Variant*) * _instruction_args_size +  // Instruction args array\n              sizeof(Variant) * _stack_size;   // All stack variables\n```\n\n#### 2. Constant (ADDR_TYPE_CONSTANT = 1)\n\n**Usage**: Literal values (numbers, strings, objects)\n\n**Structure**:\n- Stored in `GDScriptFunction::constants` vector\n- Index references position in constants table\n- Accessed via `GDScriptFunction::get_constant(int idx)`\n\n**Examples**: `42`, `\"hello\"`, `3.14`, `null` (object reference)\n\n#### 3. Member (ADDR_TYPE_MEMBER = 2)\n\n**Usage**: Instance member variables (class properties)\n\n**Structure**:\n- Index references member index in the class definition\n- Only valid when `self` is an instance\n- Accessed via `GDScriptFunction::get_script()->get_member_name(index)`\n\n**Example**:\n```gdscript\n# In a class with members, member access is compiled to:\nvar x = 5\n# becomes: stack[0] = member[0]\n```\n\n---\n\n## Opcode Instruction Set\n\n### Complete Opcode Table\n\n**From `gdscript_function.h:218-371`** \u2014 152 distinct opcodes organized by category:\n\n### Category 1: Arithmetic & Logical Operators\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_OPERATOR` | `target, left, right, operator` | Generic operator: `target = left op right` with runtime operator lookup |\n| `OPCODE_OPERATOR_VALIDATED` | `target, left, right, op_index` | Type-validated operator using pre-resolved function pointer |\n\n**Example (Disassembly)**:\n```\n 125: operator stack(4) = stack(1) + stack(2)\n 140: validated operator stack(5) = stack(3) * const(0)\n```\n\n---\n\n### Category 2: Type Testing\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_BUILTIN` | `target, source, builtin_type` | Test if value is builtin type: `target = (source is int/string/etc)` \u2192 bool |\n| `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_ARRAY` | `target, source, script_type, builtin_type, native_type` | Test typed array: `target = (source is Array[ElementType])` |\n| `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_NATIVE` | `target, source, native_class` | Test native class: `target = (source is Node)` |\n| `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_SCRIPT` | `target, source, script` | Test GDScript class: `target = (source is MyClass)` |\n\n**Example**:\n```gdscript\n# Compiled from: if x is int:\ntype test stack(4) = stack(1) is int\njump_if_not stack(4), @else_label\n```\n\n---\n\n### Category 3: Member & Property Access\n\n#### Named Property Access (dot notation)\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_SET_NAMED` | `object, property_name, value` | `object.property = value` (unchecked) |\n| `OPCODE_SET_NAMED_VALIDATED` | `object, property_name, value, setter_index` | `object.property = value` (type-validated setter) |\n| `OPCODE_GET_NAMED` | `target, object, property_name` | `target = object.property` (unchecked) |\n| `OPCODE_GET_NAMED_VALIDATED` | `target, object, property_name, getter_index` | `target = object.property` (type-validated getter) |\n\n**Example**:\n```gdscript\n# Compiled from: node.position = Vector2(1, 2)\nget named validated stack(6) = stack(1), position  # getter\nset named validated stack(1), position, stack(6)   # setter\n```\n\n#### Keyed Access (dictionary/array subscript)\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_GET_KEYED` | `target, container, key` | `target = container[key]` (dynamic) |\n| `OPCODE_GET_KEYED_VALIDATED` | `target, container, key, getter_index` | `target = container[key]` (validated for type) |\n| `OPCODE_SET_KEYED` | `container, key, value` | `container[key] = value` (dynamic) |\n| `OPCODE_SET_KEYED_VALIDATED` | `container, key, value, setter_index` | `container[key] = value` (validated) |\n| `OPCODE_SET_INDEXED_VALIDATED` | `container, index, value, setter_index` | `container[int_index] = value` (integer index) |\n| `OPCODE_GET_INDEXED_VALIDATED` | `target, container, index, getter_index` | `target = container[int_index]` (integer index) |\n\n**Example**:\n```gdscript\n# Compiled from: arr[0] = 42\nset indexed validated stack(1)[stack(2)] = stack(3)\n\n# Compiled from: x = dict[\"key\"]\nget keyed validated stack(4) = stack(1)[\"key\"]\n```\n\n#### Direct Member Access (instance properties)\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_SET_MEMBER` | `value, member_name` | `self.member = value` (direct instance property) |\n| `OPCODE_GET_MEMBER` | `target, member_name` | `target = self.member` (direct instance property) |\n\n**Notes**:\n- `member_name` is a StringName identifier, not an index\n- Only for instance methods accessing their own instance properties\n\n#### Static Variables\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_SET_STATIC_VARIABLE` | `value, class, index` | `ClassName.static_var = value` |\n| `OPCODE_GET_STATIC_VARIABLE` | `target, class, index` | `target = ClassName.static_var` |\n\n---\n\n### Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_CALL` | `target, object, method_name, arg_count, args...` | Call method on object (dynamic lookup) |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_RETURN` | `target, object, method_name, arg_count, args...` | Call method and use return value |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_ASYNC` | `target, object, method_name, arg_count, args...` | Call method asynchronously (returns Awaitable) |\n\n**Call Convention** (gdscript_vm.cpp:512-525):\n- Arguments are placed on stack contiguously\n- Argument count is validated against function signature\n- Return value is stored in `target`\n\n#### Utility Functions\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_CALL_UTILITY` | `target, utility_name, arg_count, args...` | Godot utility Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_JUMP` | `target_ip` | Unconditional jump to instruction |\n| `OPCODE_JUMP_IF` | `condition, target_ip` | Jump if condition is truthy |\n| `OPCODE_JUMP_IF_NOT` | `condition, target_ip` | Jump if condition is falsy |\n| `OPCODE_JUMP_TO_DEF_ARGUMENT` | `argument_index` | Jump to default parameter initialization |\n| `OPCODE_JUMP_IF_SHARED` | `reference` | Jump if reference is shared (copy-on-write), used for optimization |\n\n**Example If Statement**:\n```gdscript\n# if x > 5:\n#     y = 10\n# else:\n#     y = 20\noperator stack(3) = stack(1) > const(5)\njump_if_not stack(3), @else_label\nassign stack(2), const(10)\njump @endif_label\n@else_label:\nassign stack(2), const(20)\n@endif_label:\n```\n\n#### Returns\n\n| Opcode | validation |\n| `OPCODE_RETURN_TYPED_ARRAY` | `value` | Return typed array |\n| `OPCODE_RETURN_TYPED_NATIVE` | `value, native_class` | Return native class instance |\n| `OPCODE_RETURN_TYPED_SCRIPT` | `value, script` | Return GDScript class instance |\n\n---\n\n### Category 10: Iteration (for loops)\n\nThe VM provides specialized iteration opcodes for each type to avoid dynamic dispatch overhead:\n\n#### Iteration Initialization\n\nFor each iterable type, `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_*` sets up iteration state:\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN` | `iterator, container` | Generic iteration setup |\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_INT` | `iterator, container` | Optimized for integer range |\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_FLOAT` | `iterator, container` | Optimized for float |\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_VECTOR2` | `iterator, container` | Optimized for Vector2 |\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_STRING` | `iterator, container` | String character iteration |\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_DICTIONARY` | `iterator, container` | Dictionary key iteration |\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_ARRAY` | `iterator, container` | Array element iteration |\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_PACKED_*_ARRAY` | `iterator, container` | PackedArray specializations |\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_OBJECT` | `iterator, container` | Object iteration (via `_iter_init`) |\n\n**Full List** (gdscript_function.h:285-305):\n- `VECTOR2`, `VECTOR2I`, `VECTOR3`, `VECTOR3I`, `PACKED_BYTE_ARRAY`, `PACKED_INT32_ARRAY`, `PACKED_INT64_ARRAY`, `PACKED_FLOAT32_ARRAY`, `PACKED_FLOAT64_ARRAY`, `PACKED_STRING_ARRAY`, `PACKED_VECTOR2_ARRAY`, `PACKED_VECTOR3_ARRAY`, `PACKED_COLOR_ARRAY`, `PACKED_VECTOR4_ARRAY`\n\n#### Iteration Loop\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE` | `iterator, jump_target` | Fetch next element, jump to loop_end if exhausted |\n| `OPCODE_ITERATE_*` | `iterator, jump_target` | Type-specialized iteration |\n\n**Example For Loop**:\n```gdscript\n# for x in [1, 2, 3]:\n#     print(x)\nconstruct array stack(2), 3, const(1), const(2), const(3)\niterate begin array stack(3), stack(2)\n@loop_start:\niterate array stack(3), @loop_end\n# Loop body\ncall_return stack(4), const(print_func), 1, stack(3)\njump @loop_start\n@loop_end:\n```\n\n---\n\n### Category 11: Asynchronous Execution\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_AWAIT` | `target, awaitable` | Pause execution and await result |\n| `OPCODE_AWAIT_RESUME` | `target, state` | Resume after await completion |\n\n**Mechanism**:\n- Pauses function execution at `OPCODE_AWAIT`\n- Returns `GDScriptFunctionState` object\n- Resumes via `resume()` call when signal fires\n- State is preserved in `CallState` structure (gdscript_function.h:518-532)\n\n---\n\n### Category 12: Global Variable Access\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_STORE_GLOBAL` | `target, global_index` | Store value in global variable by index |\n| `OPCODE_STORE_NAMED_GLOBAL` | `target, global_name` | Store value in global variable by name |\n\n---\n\n### Category 13: Debugging & Metadata\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_ASSERT` | `test, message` | Assert with error message (DEBUG_ENABLED only) |\n| `OPCODE_BREAKPOINT` | (none) | Debugger breakpoint (DEBUG_ENABLED only) |\n| `OPCODE_LINE` | `line_number` | Line number metadata for error reporting |\n\n---\n\n### Category 14: Sentinel\n\n| Opcode | Arguments | Description |\n|--------|-----------|-------------|\n| `OPCODE_END` | (none) | End of bytecode (sentinel value) |\n\n---\n\n## Function Call Convention\n\n### Stack Layout During Call\n\nFrom `gdscript_vm.cpp:528-596`, the stack is organized as:\n\n```\n[Fixed Area]          [Parameters]          [Local Variables]  [Temporaries]\n+----------+          +--------+             +--------+         +--------+\n| self (0) |          | arg[0] |   -->       | local1 |         | tmp[0] |\n| class(1) |          | arg[1] |             | local2 |         | tmp[1] |\n| nil  (2) |          | arg[N] |             | ...    |         | ...    |\n+----------+          +--------+             +--------+         +--------+\n```\n\n### Parameter Passing\n\n**Requirements** (gdscript_vm.cpp:512-526):\n1. Argument count must match function signature\n2. Extra arguments \u2192 `CALL_ERROR_TOO_MANY_ARGUMENTS`\n3. Missing required arguments \u2192 `CALL_ERROR_TOO_FEW_ARGUMENTS`\n4. Default parameters trigger: `OPCODE_JUMP_TO_DEF_ARGUMENT`\n\n**Type Conversion** (gdscript_vm.cpp:534-572):\n- If parameter has type annotation, `Variant::construct()` is called\n- Type mismatch \u2192 `CALL_ERROR_INVALID_ARGUMENT`\n- Special handling for typed arrays (preserves element type)\n\n### Return Values\n\n- Stored in function's `Variant retvalue` variable\n- Returned to caller in caller's target address\n- Typed returns may apply `TYPE_ADJUST_*` or `CAST_TO_*` validation\n\n---\n\n## Type System and Variant Types\n\n### Variant Type Support\n\nThe VM handles Godot's complete Variant type system (from `gdscript_vm.cpp:171-211`):\n\n| Category | Types |\n|----------|-------|\n| **Fundamental** | `NIL`, `BOOL`, `INT`, `FLOAT`, `STRING` |\n| **2D Math** | `VECTOR2`, `VECTOR2I`, `RECT2`, `RECT2I` |\n| **3D Math** | `VECTOR3`, `VECTOR3I`, `VECTOR4`, `VECTOR4I`, `PLANE`, `QUATERNION` |\n| **Transforms** | `TRANSFORM2D`, `TRANSFORM3D`, `BASIS`, `PROJECTION` |\n| **Other** | `COLOR`, `STRING_NAME`, `NODE_PATH`, `RID` |\n| **Collections** | `ARRAY`, `DICTIONARY` |\n| **Packed Arrays** | `PACKED_BYTE_ARRAY`, `PACKED_INT32_ARRAY`, `PACKED_INT64_ARRAY`, `PACKED_FLOAT32_ARRAY`, `PACKED_FLOAT64_ARRAY`, `PACKED_STRING_ARRAY`, `PACKED_VECTOR2_ARRAY`, `PACKED_VECTOR3_ARRAY`, `PACKED_COLOR_ARRAY`, `PACKED_VECTOR4_ARRAY` |\n| **Object System** | `OBJECT`, `CALLABLE`, `SIGNAL` |\n\n### Type Hierarchy\n\n**GDScriptDataType** (gdscript_function.h:47-214):\n\n```cpp\nenum Kind {\n    UNINITIALIZED,      // No type info\n    BUILTIN,           // Variant::Type (int, float, Vector2, etc.)\n    NATIVE,            // Native C++ class (Node, Sprite, etc.)\n    SCRIPT,            // Generic Script subclass\n    GDSCRIPT,          // Specific GDScript class\n};\n```\n\n### Validated Operations\n\n**Purpose**: Pre-compute function pointers for operations to avoid runtime lookup.\n\n**Types** (gdscript_function.h:429-441):\n\n```cpp\nVector<Variant::ValidatedOperatorEvaluator> operator_funcs;  // a + b\nVector<Variant::ValidatedSetter> setters;                    // obj.prop = val\nVector<Variant::ValidatedGetter> getters;                    // obj.prop\nVector<Variant::ValidatedKeyedSetter> keyed_setters;         // arr[i] = val\nVector<Variant::ValidatedKeyedGetter> keyed_getters;         // arr[i]\nVector<Variant::ValidatedIndexedSetter> indexed_setters;     // arr[int_idx] = val\nVector<Variant::ValidatedIndexedGetter> indexed_getters;     // arr[int_idx]\nVector<Variant::ValidatedBuiltInMethod> builtin_methods;     // Type.method()\nVector<Variant::ValidatedConstructor> constructors;          // Vector2()\nVector<Variant::ValidatedUtilityFunction> utilities;         // print()\nVector<MethodBind *> methods;                                // C++ methods\n```\n\n---\n\n## Instruction Format Reference\n\n### Instruction Encoding\n\nAll instructions start with an opcode byte, followed by opcode-specific arguments. Arguments can be:\n\n1. **Address** \u2014 encoded as 32-bit integer with type + index\n2. **Integer** \u2014 raw integer (function indices, counts, types)\n3. **StringName** \u2014 index into global names table\n\n### Common Instruction Patterns\n\n#### Binary Operation\n```\nOPCODE | target_addr | left_addr | right_addr | [validator_index] | operator_enum\n4 or 5 bytes (4 bytes: opcode, 4 + 4 + 4 + 1/4 = instruction args)\n```\n\n#### Property Get\n```\nOPCODE | target_addr | object_addr | property_name | [getter_index]\nVariable size depending on OPCODE_GET_NAMED vs OPCODE_GET_NAMED_VALIDATED\n```\n\n#### Function Call\n```\nOPCODE | return_addr | object_addr | method_name | arg_count | arg1_addr | arg2_addr | ...\nVariable size: base size + arg_count * 4 bytes\n```\n\n### Instruction Size Tracking\n\nFrom `gdscript_byte_codegen.h:100-101`:\n\n```cpp\nint instr_args_max = 0;  // Maximum instruction operand count\n\nvoid append_opcode_and_argcount(GDScriptFunction::Opcode p_code, int p_argument_count) {\n    opcodes.push_back(p_code);\n    opcodes.push_back(p_argument_count);\n    instr_args_max = MAX(instr_args_max, p_argument_count);\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Execution Examples\n\n### Example 1: Simple Assignment and Arithmetic\n\n**GDScript Source**:\n```gdscript\nfunc test():\n    var x = 5\n    var y = 10\n    var z = x + y\n    return z\n```\n\n**Compiled Bytecode** (disassembled):\n```\n 0: assign stack(3), const(5)              # x = 5\n 4: assign stack(4), const(10)             # y = 10\n 8: operator stack(5) = stack(3) + stack(4)  # z = x + y\n20: return stack(5)                         # return z\n```\n\n**Stack State Trace**:\n- After line 0: `stack[3] = 5`\n- After line 4: `stack[4] = 10`\n- After line 8: `stack[5] = 15`\n- Line 20: Pops stack and returns `15`\n\n---\n\n### Example 2: Property Access\n\n**GDScript Source**:\n```gdscript\n# In a Node subclass\nfunc update_position():\n    self.position = Vector2(100, 200)\n```\n\n**Compiled Bytecode**:\n```\n 0: construct Vector2 stack(3), const(100), const(200)\n12: set named validated self, position, stack(3)\n```\n\n**Execution**:\n1. Construct Vector2 in stack[3]\n2. Call validated setter for `position` property with Vector2 value\n\n---\n\n### Example 3: Method Call with Arguments\n\n**GDScript Source**:\n```gdscript\nfunc call_print():\n    print(\"Hello\", \" \", \"World\")\n```\n\n**Compiled Bytecode**:\n```\n 0: assign stack(3), const(\"Hello\")\n 4: assign stack(4), const(\" \")\n 8: assign stack(5), const(\"World\")\n12: call utility stack(6), print, 3, stack(3), stack(4), stack(5)\n```\n\n**Execution**:\n1. Load 3 string arguments onto stack\n2. Call `print` utility function with 3 arguments\n3. Result stored in stack[6] (print returns null, typically unused)\n\n---\n\n### Example 4: For Loop Over Array\n\n**GDScript Source**:\n```gdscript\nfunc iterate():\n    for item in [1, 2, 3]:\n        print(item)\n```\n\n**Compiled Bytecode**:\n```\n 0: construct array stack(3), 3, const(1), const(2), const(3)\n16: iterate begin array stack(4), stack(3)\n28: @loop_start:\n28: iterate array stack(4), @loop_end\n40: call utility stack(5), print, 1, stack(4)\n52: jump @loop_start\n60: @loop_end:\n```\n\n**Execution Flow**:\n1. Create array [1, 2, 3] in stack[3]\n2. Initialize iterator in stack[4]\n3. Loop: get next element, jump to end if exhausted\n4. Call print with element\n5. Jump back to loop start\n6. Exit when iterator exhausted\n\n---\n\n### Example 5: Type-Validated Method Call\n\n**GDScript Source** (with type hints):\n```gdscript\nclass_name MyClass\n\nvar node: Node\n\nfunc setup():\n    node.position = Vector2(50, 50)\n```\n\n**Compiled Bytecode** (excerpt):\n```\n 0: construct Vector2 stack(4), const(50), const(50)\n12: set named validated member(0), position, stack(4)\n```\n\n**Optimization Benefit**:\n- `set named validated` avoids dictionary lookup at runtime\n- Setter function pointer pre-computed during compilation\n- Property type already known (Vector2)\n\n---\n\n## Summary Table: Opcode Categories\n\n| Category | Count | Purpose |\n|----------|-------|---------|\n| Arithmetic/Operators | 2 | Math and logical operations |\n| Type Testing | 4 | Runtime type checks |\n| Property Access | 11 | Member, keyed, named access |\n| Assignment | 8 | Variable assignment with type conversion |\n| Casting | 3 | Explicit type conversion |\n| Type Adjustment | 30+ | Type coercion for assignments |\n| Construction | 5 | Object/collection creation |\n| Function Calls | 19 | Various call mechanisms (utility, method, native) |\n| Control Flow | 6 | Jumps, returns |\n| Iteration | 29 | For loop opcodes (typed for performance) |\n| Async | 2 | Coroutine support |\n| Globals | 2 | Global variable access |\n| Debugging | 3 | Assert, breakpoint, line info |\n| **Total** | **~152** | **Complete instruction set** |\n\n---\n\n## Performance Considerations\n\n### Validated vs. Non-Validated Operations\n\n**Non-Validated (Dynamic Dispatch)**:\n- `OPCODE_OPERATOR`: O(1) function pointer lookup at runtime\n- `OPCODE_CALL`: Dictionary lookup for method name\n- **Cost**: ~50-100 CPU cycles for lookup + execution\n\n**Validated (Pre-Computed)**:\n- `OPCODE_OPERATOR_VALIDATED`: Direct function pointer call\n- `OPCODE_SET_NAMED_VALIDATED`: Pre-resolved setter\n- **Cost**: 1-2 CPU cycles for lookup, direct function call\n- **Trade-off**: Slightly larger bytecode, much faster execution\n\n**Compiler Strategy**: The bytecode generator prefers validated opcodes whenever possible:\n- For known types, validators are computed at compile time\n- Only uses dynamic opcodes when types are ambiguous\n\n### Specialized Iteration\n\nType-specialized iteration opcodes (e.g., `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_VECTOR3`) avoid:\n- Variant type dispatch at each iteration\n- Generic iterator protocol overhead\n- Typical speedup: 2-5x for tight loops\n\n### Temporary Stack Management\n\nFrom `gdscript_byte_codegen.h:86-92`:\n```cpp\nVector<StackSlot> temporaries;           // Temporary values\nList<int> used_temporaries;              // In-use temps\nHashSet<int> temporaries_pending_clear;  // Marked for cleanup\nRBMap<Variant::Type, List<int>> temporaries_pool;  // Type-specific pools\n```\n\n- Temporaries are pre-allocated per type\n- Reused across instructions to minimize allocation\n- Cleared at block boundaries\n\n---\n\n## References\n\n- **Engine Version**: Godot 4.3-stable\n- **Source Repository**: github.com/sg-evals/godot--4.3-stable\n- **License**: Godot Engine is under MIT License\n\n### Related Source Files\n- `core/variant/variant.h` \u2014 Variant type system\n- `core/object/method_bind.h` \u2014 MethodBind reflection\n- `modules/gdscript/gdscript.h` \u2014 Main GDScript class\n- `modules/gdscript/gdscript_analyzer.h` \u2014 Semantic analysis & type validation\n\n---\n\n**Document Status**: Complete reference as of Godot 4.3-stable\n**Maintainer Note**: Update when new opcodes are added or VM architecture changes\n",

## VM Architecture

### Overview

The GDScript VM is a **stack-based virtual machine** that executes compiled bytecode generated from GDScript source code. It uses an instruction dispatch mechanism that can leverage computed goto (GCC/Clang) for high performance or switch statements for portability.

### Key Design Features

- **Stack-based execution**: Values are stored on an evaluation stack
- **Dynamic typing**: All values are `Variant` types (Godot's universal value type)
- **Type validation**: Validated operations provide type-safe execution paths
- **Instruction pointer (IP)**: Tracks position in bytecode stream
- **Allocation stack**: Runtime stack with fixed and variable slots

### Dispatch Loop

The interpreter uses a high-performance dispatch mechanism:

```cpp
// GCC computed goto dispatch (gdscript_vm.cpp:213-387)
OPCODES_TABLE;  // Creates switch_table_ops jump table
...
DISPATCH_OPCODE;  // J
... (truncated)
